{"Quotes": "", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), which is considered one of the most promising propylene production methods. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Recent research has contributed to our current knowledge of these catalysts, including the identification of [GaH]2+ together with a basic framework oxygen of the Brnsted-acid site as active sites for PDH reactions.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢（PDH），这被认为是生产丙烯最有前景的方法之一。对于Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂在PDH中的理解已经发展，关于活性Ga物种的争论仍在继续。最近的研究为这些催化剂的当前知识做出了贡献，包括识别[GaH]2+与Brnsted酸位点的基本骨架氧一起作为PDH反应的活性位点。", "Doi": "10.1021/accountsmr.0c00012"},
{"Quotes": "", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has driven the rapid application and development of propane dehydrogenation technologies. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Recent research has identified Lewis(Ga+)-Brnsted acid pairs as the active sites for propane dehydrogenation over Ga/H-ZSM-5. The increased Lewis acidity facilitates heterolytic CH bond activation, and Brnsted acidity reduces the activation barrier for the elimination of hydrogen.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了丙烷脱氢技术的快速发展。对于Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂在PDH中的活性Ga物种的理解一直在演变，存在持续的争论。最近的研究发现，Ga/H-ZSM-5上Lewis(Ga+)-Brnsted酸对是丙烷脱氢的活性位点。增加的Lewis酸性促进了CH键的异裂，而Brnsted酸性降低了氢消除的活化能。", "Doi": "10.1039/d0cs00983k"},
{"Quotes": "", "English": "The literature does not provide information on how the growing demand for propylene has influenced the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), or how the understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, including the ongoing debate about active Ga species and recent research findings that have contributed to our current knowledge of these catalysts. However, it is mentioned that Ga species in H-ZSM5 zeolites catalyze rate-limiting dehydrogenation steps during the conversion of alkanes to aromatics, promoting the recombinative desorption of H-adatoms as H2 and inhibiting undesired cracking reactions. The literature focuses on the physical and chemical state of Ga using in-situ X-ray absorption at the Ga K-edge, showing that Ga+3 species initially present in fresh catalysts reduce at temperatures below 770 K during hydrogen pretreatment or propane reactions. Reduced Ga is present in highly dispersed form without Ga nearest neighbors, probably as a monomeric hydride species coordinated to basic oxygens within zeolite channels. These hydride species are driven to release molecular hydrogen by the high surface hydrogen fugacities that develop during propane dehydrocyclodimerization on H-ZSM5. Reduced Ga species reoxidize to Ga+3 when samples are cooled to room temperature in flowing H2, suggesting that active forms of Ga exist only at reaction conditions.", "Chinese": "文献没有提供关于丙烯需求增长如何影响新生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢（PDH），以及对Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂用于PDH的理解如何演变，包括关于活性Ga物种的持续争论和最近的研究发现如何有助于我们当前对这些催化剂的理解的信息。然而，文献中提到Ga物种在H-ZSM5沸石中催化烷烃转化为芳烃过程中的脱氢步骤，促进H-原子的重组脱附为H2，同时抑制不希望发生的裂解反应。文献重点在于使用原位X射线吸收光谱在Ga K边研究Ga的物理和化学状态。新鲜催化剂中存在的Ga+3物种在770 K以下的温度下在氢预处理或丙烷反应中还原。还原的Ga以高度分散的形式存在，没有Ga最近邻，可能作为单体氢化物物种与沸石通道内的碱性氧配位。这些氢化物物种在H-ZSM5上进行丙烷脱氢环二聚化时，由于表面氢逸度的增加，被驱动释放分子氢。当样品在流动的H2中冷却至室温时，还原的Ga物种重新氧化为Ga+3，这表明活性形式的Ga仅在反应条件下存在。", "Doi": "10.1006/jcat.1993.1079"},

propylene has led to the development of new production methods, including propane dehydrogenation (PDH), to meet the projected shortfall in supply. Propylene is a key chemical used in the production of various materials, such as polypropylene, acrylonitrile, propylene oxide, and cymene. The demand for propylene is expected to increase significantly, from 130 megatons in 2019 to 191 megatons by 2030. To address this demand, on-purpose propylene technologies, including PDH, have been developed. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over time, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Ga-based catalysts have a long history in hydrocarbon processing, with the dehydroaromatization activity of supported gallium oxide being recognized in the 1970s. Since dehydrogenation is the first step in dehydroaromatization, the ability of Ga/H-ZSM-5 to dehydrogenate light alkanes to alkenes was well appreciated. However, the Ga speciation and the structure of active sites on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in dehydrogenation have remained active topics of discussion since its initial discovery without clear resolution. Different Ga species have been proposed to be the active center of the PDH, including Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaOH]2+, [GaH]2+, [GaH2]+, and Ga+H+ pair. Recent research has combined in situ transmission Fourier-transform infrared (FTIR) spectroscopy, pulse titration studies, and PDH kinetics to demonstrate that the Ga speciation and their PDH performance are dependent on both Ga/Al ratios and Al distributions of the zeolites.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，包括丙烷脱氢（PDH），以弥补预计的供应缺口。丙烯是生产各种材料的关键化学品，如聚丙烯、丙烯腈、环氧丙烷和莰烯。预计丙烯需求将大幅增加，从2019年的130百万吨增加到2030年的191百万吨。为了满足这一需求，开发了包括PDH在内的目的性丙烯技术。对Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂在PDH中的理解随着时间的推移而发展，关于活性Ga物种的争论仍在继续。基于镓的催化剂在烃加工中有着悠久的历史，早在20世纪70年代，就认识到了支撑镓氧化物的脱氢芳构化活性。由于脱氢是脱氢芳构化的第一步，Ga/H-ZSM-5将轻烷烃脱氢为烯烃的能力得到了充分的赞赏。然而，自其首次发现以来，Ga/H-ZSM-5在脱氢中的Ga物种和活性位点的结构一直是讨论的活跃话题，没有明确的结论。提出了不同的Ga物种作为PDH的活性中心，包括Ga+、[GaO]+、[Ga(OH)2]+、[GaOH]2+、[GaH]2+、[GaH2]+和Ga+H+对。最近的研究结合了原位透射傅里叶变换红外（FTIR）光谱、脉冲滴定研究和PDH动力学，证明Ga物种和它们的PDH性能取决于Ga/Al比率和沸石的Al分布。", "Doi": "10.1002/advs.202207756_0"},
{"Quotes": "Propylene plays a central role in the chemical industry infras- tructure and it is used for the production of a wide range of chem- icals, including polypropylene, acrylonitrile, propylene oxide, and cymene [1]. Propylene is currently obtained as a by-product from naphtha steam crackers and fluidized catalytic cracking (FCC) units in refineries [2]. However, there has been a growing gap between the demand and supply of propylene, due to a marked increase in the abundance of natural gas as a feedstock [3]. Propane dehy- drogenation (PDH) is potentially an effective alternative to produc- ing propylene, and two PDH processes, i.e., the Catofin process with a CrOx/Al2O3 catalyst and the Oleflex process using a Pt-based cat- alyst, have been commercialized [4,5]. The high cost of Pt and the health and environmental concerns associated with Cr, have incen- tivized development of other PDH catalysts [4], such as Ga- [612], Zn- [13], Co- [1416], V-based [17] and ZrO2 [1820] catalysts.\nAmong these, Ga/H-ZSM-5 has long been recognized as an efficient catalyst for both dehydrogenation and dehydroaromatization of alkanes (the Cyclar process), however, Ga speciation, the identity of catalytic active sites and the reaction mechanism of the PDH reaction remain topics of active discussion despite decades of research [911,2123].\nVarious experimental techniques including in-situ Ga K edge X- ray absorption near edge structure (XANES), ex-situ FTIR and NH3- temperature-programmed desorption (NH3-TPD) have been employed to probe Ga speciation in Ga/H-ZSM-5 and identify the active site in the PDH reaction [911,24].\nA number of Ga species, such as Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga (OH)]2+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaH2]+, [GaH]2+, have been proposed to form after the reduction of Ga/H-ZSM-5 based on several experimental and computational techniques [911,24,2628].\nEarly in-situ X-ray absorption study showed that isolated Ga+ ions are the main species in Ga/H-ZSM-5 independent of the gallium loading and the utilized reducing gas [24,29], which is consistent with a more recent report by Schreiber et al. [10] Alternative interpretations of edge shifts in Ga K-edge XANES spectra acquired under reaction conditions have been proposed, as XANES spectra are not suffi- ciently resolved to differentiate Ga+ from low-coordinate Ga-alkyl or hydride species [11,30].\nHensen and coworkers [27,28] first identified Ga monohydride and dihydride species on reduced Ga/ H-ZSM-5 with diffuse reflectance infrared Fourier Transform spec- troscopy (DRIFTS), suggesting that these species could play an active role in the PDH.\nHowever, they collected spectra at room temperature after reducing samples with H2 at 500 C, and the state of the catalyst at room temperature after cooling may not be representative of the catalyst state at 500 C.\nRecently, Phadke et al. [9] proposed that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active centers for the PDH reaction, and the catalysts reactivity is independent of Ga/Al ratio.\nThis was supported by FTIR spectroscopic and NH3-TPD results, along with thermodynamic stability analysis [11].\nFTIR and NH3-TPD experiments in these studies were con- ducted on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in its oxidized state [11], where the Ga spe- ciation could be quite different from that of the reduced sample.\nSchreiber et al. [10] reported that the Ga+H+ paired sites were more active than single Ga+ sites and the parent H-ZSM-5 catalyst based on a combination of reactivity, quantitative pulse reactions,and DFT calculations.\nThe hypothesis of Ga+H+ pair sites and iso- lated Ga+ species having different reactivities has been put forth in recent investigations by both the Bell and the Lercher groups [9 11,21], however, the existence of these distinct sites is largely indi- rect; inferred from reactivity data, indirect experimental character- izations and computational investigations.", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to a gap between demand and supply, as propylene is traditionally obtained as a by-product from naphtha steam crackers and fluidized catalytic cracking units in refineries. The abundance of natural gas as a feedstock has exacerbated this gap. Propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is seen as a potentially effective alternative method to produce propylene. Two commercialized PDH processes are the Catofin process using a CrOx/Al2O3 catalyst and the Oleflex process with a Pt-based catalyst. However, the high cost of Pt and health and environmental concerns associated with Cr have driven the development of alternative PDH catalysts, such as Ga-, Zn-, Co-, V-based, and ZrO2 catalysts. Among these, Ga/H-ZSM-5 has been recognized as an efficient catalyst for dehydrogenation and dehydroaromatization of alkanes, but the identity of catalytic active sites and the reaction mechanism of PDH remain topics of active discussion. Various experimental techniques, including in-situ Ga K edge X-ray absorption near edge structure (XANES), ex-situ FTIR, and NH3-temperature-programmed desorption (NH3-TPD), have been used to probe Ga speciation in Ga/H-ZSM-5 and identify the active site in PDH. A number of Ga species have been proposed to form after the reduction of Ga/H-ZSM-5, including Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga(OH)]2+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaH2]+, and [GaH]2+. Early X-ray absorption studies suggested that isolated Ga+ ions are the main species in Ga/H-ZSM-5, independent of gallium loading and reducing gas, consistent with a recent report. However, alternative interpretations of edge shifts in Ga K-edge XANES spectra have been proposed, as XANES spectra are not sufficiently resolved to differentiate Ga+ from low-coordinate Ga-alkyl or hydride species. Hensen and coworkers first identified Ga monohydride and dihydride species on reduced Ga/H-ZSM-5 using diffuse reflectance infrared Fourier Transform spectroscopy (DRIFTS), suggesting these species could play an active role in PDH. However, spectra were collected at room temperature after reducing samples with H2 at 500 C, which may not represent the catalyst state at 500 C. Phadke et al. proposed that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active centers for PDH, and catalyst reactivity is independent of Ga/Al ratio, supported by FTIR spectroscopic, NH3-TPD results, and thermodynamic stability analysis. However, FTIR and NH3-TPD experiments were conducted on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in its oxidized state, where Ga speciation could differ from the reduced sample. Schreiber et al. reported that Ga+H+ paired sites were more active than single Ga+ sites and the parent H-ZSM-5 catalyst based on reactivity, quantitative pulse reactions, and DFT calculations. The hypothesis of Ga+H+ pair sites and isolated Ga+ species having different reactivities has been put forth in recent investigations, but the existence of these distinct sites is largely indirect, inferred from reactivity data, indirect experimental characterizations, and computational investigations.", "Chinese": "丙烯在化工基础设施中扮演着核心角色，用于生产包括聚丙烯、丙烯腈、丙烯氧化物和莰烯在内的广泛化学品。目前，丙烯作为副产品，主要来自炼油厂的石脑油蒸汽裂解和流化催化裂解（FCC）单元。然而，由于天然气作为原料的显著增加，丙烯的需求和供应之间出现了日益扩大的差距。丙烷脱氢（PDH）被认为是一种生产丙烯的有效替代方法，两种PDH工艺，即使用CrOx/Al2O3催化剂的Catofin工艺和使用基于Pt的催化剂的Oleflex工艺，已被商业化。然而，由于Pt的高成本以及与Cr相关的健康和环境问题，这推动了其他PDH催化剂的发展，如Ga-、Zn-、Co-、V基和ZrO2催化剂。其中，Ga/H-ZSM-5长期以来被公认为是烷烃脱氢和脱氢芳构化（Cyclar工艺）的有效催化剂，然而，Ga的物种化、催化活性位点的身份以及PDH反应的反应机制仍然是几十年研究的活跃讨论话题。包括原位Ga K边X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）、原位FTIR和NH3-温度程序脱附（NH3-TPD）在内的各种实验技术已被用于探究Ga/H-ZSM-5中的Ga物种化并识别PDH反应中的活性位点。根据几种实验和计算技术，提出了在Ga/H-ZSM-5还原后可能形成的Ga物种，如Ga+、[GaO]+、[Ga(OH)]2+、[Ga(OH)2]+、[GaH2]+和[GaH]2+。早期的X射线吸收研究表明，无论镓的负载量和所用还原气体如何，孤立的Ga+离子是Ga/H-ZSM-5中的主要物种，这与Schreiber等人最近的报告一致。然而，对在反应条件下获得的Ga K边XANES光谱的边缘位移的替代解释已被提出，因为XANES光谱不足以区分Ga+和低配位Ga-烷基或氢化物物种。Hensen及其同事首先使用扩散反射红外傅里叶变换光谱（DRIFTS）在还原的Ga/H-ZSM-5上识别了Ga单氢化物和二氢化物物种，表明这些物种可能在PDH中发挥活性作用。然而，他们在用H2在500°C还原样品后，在室温下收集光谱，而催化剂在室温下的状态可能无法代表500°C时的催化剂状态。Phadke等人最近提出，单个[GaH]2+位点是PDH反应的活性中心，催化剂的活性独立于Ga/Al比。这得到了FTIR光谱、NH3-TPD结果以及热力学稳定性分析的支持。然而，这些研究中的FTIR和NH3-TPD实验是在Ga/H-ZSM-5的氧化状态下进行的，其中Ga的物种化可能与还原样品大不相同。Schreiber等人报告说，Ga+H+配对位点比单个Ga+位点和母体H-ZSM-5催化剂更活跃，这是基于反应性、定量脉冲反应和DFT计算的组合。Ga+H+配对位点和孤立Ga+物种具有不同反应性的假设在Bell和Lercher小组的最近调查中被提出，然而，这些不同位点的存在在很大程度上是间接的，从反应性数据、间接实验表征和计算研究中推断出来。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2020.11.004"},

{"Quotes": "[1] \"The active sites for PDH in Ga/H-ZSM-5 with medium quantities of tetrahedral aluminum in the lattice were distinguished to be LewisBrnsted acid pairs.102 The [GaH]2+, together with a basic framework oxygen of the Brnsted-acid site, heterolyti- cally activates a propane CH bond with a very low intrinsic enthalpy barrier of 56 kJ mol1. This LewisBrnsted acid pair turned out to be far more active than an isolated Ga+, which can be attributed to the increasing Lewis acidity upon protonation of Ga+ by the Brnsted acid site which promotes heterolytic CH bond activation (Fig. 18h). Besides, the Brnsted acid site prominently detruncates the activation barrier for H2 elimina- tion which is considerably high for the isolated Ga+ because the proton originates from an alkyl CH bond with the simulta- neous elimination of propene.\"\n          [1] \"Propylene is an important building block for enormous petrochemicals including polypropylene,propylene oxide, acrylonitrile and so forth. They found that the promoter of Pt helps in facilitating hydrogen desorption and recovering the gallium hydride and/or hydroxide species.\"\n          [1] \"Propylene is the basic raw material for the production of acrolein, polypropylene, acetone, acrylonitrile, propylene oxide and other industrial products.1 Conventional propylene pro- duction processes involve fluid catalytic cracking, and steam cracking of naphtha and light diesel. However, with the rapid consumption of fossil energy, traditional propylene production methods can no longer meet the increasing demands. Therefore,the development of highly efficient propylene production technologies is of vital importance, both scientifically and economically.2 In the past few years, increasing technologies for propylene production have been widely developed, such as propane dehydrogenation (PDH), the methanol-to-olefins (MTO) process, and the FischerTropsch-to-olefins process (Fig. 1a and b). {"Quotes": "No quotes provided", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to increased attention on the catalytic dehydrogenation of propane to propylene, as conventional hydrocarbon steam cracking and catalytic cracking processes cannot meet the growing demand. Gallium oxide-based catalysts, including Ga/H-ZSM-5, have been recognized as promising materials for alkane dehydrogenation due to their capability to activate hydrocarbon species and excellent catalytic efficiency. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Recent research has shown that the existence of strong acid sites in the catalyst can lead to more well-dispersed Ga species, which is beneficial for the propane dehydrogenation reaction. The 5Ga2O3/ZSM-5 sample exhibits the highest catalytic activity, possessing the maximum well-dispersed gallium species and high dehydrogenation efficiency gallium ions (Gad+ cations, d < 2). The 5Ga2O3/SBA-15 catalyst exhibits the highest catalytic stability. The support effects of catalysts were also considered to be an important topic. Previous studies reported that the Ga2O3 species were dispersed on different supports including TiO2, MgO, Al2O3, ZrO2, ZSM-5, HZSM-48 and MWW zeolites for alkane dehydrogenation reaction. Many literatures verified that acidity of support evidently influenced the catalytic performance of the supported catalysts. The detailed investigations of different supports on the catalytic performances for Ga2O3-based catalysts are rarely reported, especially with SBA-15 material as support. activation.\"\n          [12] \"The BAS also significantly reduces the activation barrier for H2 elimination by recombination with a hydride.\"", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), as an alternative to traditional steam cracking and fluid catalytic cracking. The discovery of active and selective catalysts is central to the development of these on-purpose technologies. Research into propane dehydrogenation is an ever-growing field, with several review articles available on direct dehydrogenation (DDH), soft oxidation with CO2 (ODH-CO2), and oxidative dehydrogenation (ODH-O2). The scope of this article is to critically review the literature on DDH, ODH-CO2, and ODH-O2 to identify overarching themes and common rules for catalyst design. The environmental and economic aspects of different existing propene production technologies are important considerations when reviewing the feasibility of newer technologies based on dehydrogenation. Green chemistry principles, such as atom economy, the use of toxic chemicals, and the renewability of the feedstock, are especially relevant. The increased interest in direct propane dehydrogenation has been enhanced by the fall in propane price, which is the direct result of the discovery of vast shale gas reserves in North America. Although propane is a minor component in shale gas, it is facile to separate and therefore represents a valuable, but non-renewable source of propane. Increasing public pressure to move away from such non-renewable feedstocks continues to gain momentum, and the propane production industry has responded accordingly. The production of renewable green propane (also called bio-propane and bioLPG) is an emerging sector which is already being operated on a large scale. TotalEnergies operates a bio-refinery in La Mede, which has a design capacity for bio-propane of 25000 tonnes per year. Additionally, Neste recently opened a renewable propane production plant, which will produce 40000 tonnes per year. The propane generated is then sold on to be used in direct propane dehydrogenation. While this is an important start, it represents less than 1% of annual propane capacity. Bio-propane can be produced from the processing of biomass, notably as a side-product in the production of bio-diesel as well as glycerol and other substrates. With increasing pressure to source chemical feedstocks sustainably, we can expect that new interest will focus on renewable and green routes to the key platform chemicals currently required by modern society, and that green propane will play an important role in this. Overall, direct propane dehydrogenation satisfies many principles of green chemistry in comparison to SC and MTO benchmarks: it is highly atom-economic, does not use toxic reactants (or generate toxic by-products) and can in principle, utilise renewable feedstocks. However, in practice dehydrogenation will only be desirable as a means of producing propene if the reaction can operate efficiently, with minimal side-products and maximum yield. These factors are governed by the choice of catalyst, the main focus of the current review. The development of an active, selective and stable catalyst is essential for dehydrogenation to be considered as a viable process in the near- and long-term future.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢（PDH），作为传统蒸汽裂解和流化催化裂解的替代方案。发现活性和选择性催化剂是开发这些目的技术的核心。丙烷脱氢的研究是一个不断增长的领域，目前有几篇关于直接脱氢（DDH）、二氧化碳软氧化（ODH-CO2）和氧化脱氢（ODH-O2）的综述文章。本文的范围是批判性地回顾DDH、ODH-CO2和ODH-O2的文献，以确定催化剂设计的总体主题和共同规则。我们不试图捕捉反应设计和工程的方面，这本身是一个充满活力的研究领域。我们试图通过计算空间时间产率（STY）（以molC3H6 kgcat1 h1为单位）来比较不同子反应中催化剂的性能，这是基于催化剂的初始活性。此外，我们强调了每个反应的环境和工业视角以及工业应用的前景。不同现有丙烯生产技术的环境和经济方面在审查基于脱氢的较新技术的可行性时是重要的考虑因素。绿色化学原则，如原子经济性、有毒化学品的使用和原料的可再生性，尤其相关。直接丙烷脱氢与SC和MTO基准相比，在绿色化学的许多原则方面令人满意：它是高度原子经济的，不使用有毒反应物（或产生有毒副产品），原则上可以利用可再生原料。然而，在实践中，只有当反应能够有效运行，具有最小的副产品和最大产量时，脱氢才是一种理想的丙烯生产方式。这些因素受催化剂选择的支配，这是当前综述的主要焦点。开发活性、选择性和稳定的催化剂对于脱氢在近期和长期未来被视为可行的过程至关重要。", "Doi": "10.1039/d1gc03700e"},
{"Quotes": "", "English": "The increasing world demand for propylene and the current low cost of propane derived from shale gas have renewed interest in the propane dehydrogenation reaction (PDH). {"Quotes": "", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), as an alternative to traditional methods such as steam cracking. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over time, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Recent research has contributed to our current knowledge of these catalysts, including the identification of coordinatively unsaturated tetrahedral Ga3+ cations as the active sites for dehydrogenation activity. However, the exact nature of the active sites is still under debate, with some authors proposing the presence of Lewis acid sites, while others suggest the involvement of both Lewis and Brnsted acid sites. The role of CO2 in improving olefin yields has also been studied, with various mechanisms proposed, including the removal of acid sites, coke gasification, and hydrogen removal by the reverse water-gas shift reaction. The addition of promoters, such as potassium, has been shown to reduce coke formation and increase selectivity. The reducibility of Ga2O3 and the effect of hydrogen and steam on the catalyst's activity have also been investigated. The promotion of GaOx-based dehydrogenation catalysts with metals like Pt has been reported to assist hydrogen desorption and facilitate the regeneration of active sites.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢(PDH)，作为传统方法如蒸汽裂解的替代。对于PDH中Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂的理解随着时间的推移而发展，关于活性Ga物种的争论仍在继续。最近的研究为这些催化剂的当前知识做出了贡献，包括确定四面体配位不足的Ga3+阳离子作为脱氢活性位点。然而，活性位点的确切性质仍在争论中，一些作者提出存在Lewis酸位点，而另一些则建议涉及Lewis和Brnsted酸位点。关于CO2提高烯烃产率的作用也进行了研究，提出了各种机制，包括去除酸位点、焦炭气化和通过逆水煤气变换反应去除氢气。添加钾等促进剂已被证明可以减少焦炭形成并提高选择性。Ga2O3的还原性和氢气、蒸汽对催化剂活性的影响也进行了研究。据报道，Pt等金属对GaOx基脱氢催化剂的促进作用有助于氢气解吸，促进活性位点的再生。", "Doi": "10.1021/cr5002436"},

{"Quotes": "", "English": "The literature does not provide information on how the growing demand for propylene has influenced the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), or how the understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, including the ongoing debate about active Ga species and recent research findings that have contributed to our current knowledge of these catalysts. However, it is mentioned that Ga species in H-ZSM5 zeolites catalyze rate-limiting dehydrogenation steps during the conversion of alkanes to aromatics, promoting the recombinative desorption of H-adatoms as H2 and inhibiting undesired cracking reactions. The literature focuses on the physical and chemical state of Ga using in-situ X-ray absorption at the Ga K-edge, showing that Ga+3 species initially present in fresh catalysts reduce at temperatures below 770 K during hydrogen pretreatment or propane reactions. Reduced Ga is present in highly dispersed form without Ga nearest neighbors, probably as a monomeric hydride species coordinated to basic oxygens within zeolite channels. These hydride species are driven to release molecular hydrogen by the high surface hydrogen fugacities that develop during propane dehydrocyclodimerization on H-ZSM5. propylene has led to the development of new production methods, including propane dehydrogenation (PDH), to meet the projected shortfall in supply. Propylene is a key chemical used in the production of various materials, such as polypropylene, acrylonitrile, propylene oxide, and cymene. The demand for propylene is expected to increase significantly, from 130 megatons in 2019 to 191 megatons by 2030. To address this demand, on-purpose propylene technologies, including PDH, have been developed. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over time, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Ga-based catalysts have a long history in hydrocarbon processing, with the dehydroaromatization activity of supported gallium oxide being recognized in the 1970s. Since dehydrogenation is the first step in dehydroaromatization, the ability of Ga/H-ZSM-5 to dehydrogenate light alkanes to alkenes was well appreciated. {"Quotes": "Propylene plays a central role in the chemical industry infras- tructure and it is used for the production of a wide range of chem- icals, including polypropylene, acrylonitrile, propylene oxide, and cymene [1]. Propylene is currently obtained as a by-product from naphtha steam crackers and fluidized catalytic cracking (FCC) units in refineries [2]. However, there has been a growing gap between the demand and supply of propylene, due to a marked increase in the abundance of natural gas as a feedstock [3]. Propane dehy- drogenation (PDH) is potentially an effective alternative to produc- ing propylene, and two PDH processes, i.e., the Catofin process with a CrOx/Al2O3 catalyst and the Oleflex process using a Pt-based cat- alyst, have been commercialized [4,5]. The high cost of Pt and the health and environmental concerns associated with Cr, have incen- tivized development of other PDH catalysts [4], such as Ga- [612], Zn- [13], Co- [1416], V-based [17] and ZrO2 [1820] catalysts.\nAmong these, Ga/H-ZSM-5 has long been recognized as an efficient catalyst for both dehydrogenation and dehydroaromatization of alkanes (the Cyclar process), however, Ga speciation, the identity of catalytic active sites and the reaction mechanism of the PDH reaction remain topics of active discussion despite decades of research [911,2123].\nVarious experimental techniques including in-situ Ga K edge X- ray absorption near edge structure (XANES), ex-situ FTIR and NH3- temperature-programmed desorption (NH3-TPD) have been employed to probe Ga speciation in Ga/H-ZSM-5 and identify the active site in the PDH reaction [911,24].\nA number of Ga species, such as Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga (OH)]2+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaH2]+, [GaH]2+, have been proposed to form after the reduction of Ga/H-ZSM-5 based on several experimental and computational techniques [911,24,2628].\nEarly in-situ X-ray absorption study showed that isolated Ga+ ions are the main species in Ga/H-ZSM-5 independent of the gallium loading and the utilized reducing gas [24,29], which is consistent with a more recent report by Schreiber et al. [10] Alternative interpretations of edge shifts in Ga K-edge XANES spectra acquired under reaction conditions have been proposed, as XANES spectra are not suffi- ciently resolved to differentiate Ga+ from low-coordinate Ga-alkyl or hydride species [11,30].\nHensen and coworkers [27,28] first identified Ga monohydride and dihydride species on reduced Ga/ H-ZSM-5 with diffuse reflectance infrared Fourier Transform spec- troscopy (DRIFTS), suggesting that these species could play an active role in the PDH.\nHowever, they collected spectra at room temperature after reducing samples with H2 at 500 C, and the state of the catalyst at room temperature after cooling may not be representative of the catalyst state at 500 C.\nRecently, Phadke et al. [9] proposed that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active centers for the PDH reaction, and the catalysts reactivity is independent of Ga/Al ratio.\nThis was supported by FTIR spectroscopic and NH3-TPD results, along with thermodynamic stability analysis [11].\nFTIR and NH3-TPD experiments in these studies were con- ducted on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in its oxidized state [11], where the Ga spe- ciation could be quite different from that of the reduced sample.\nSchreiber et al. [10] reported that the Ga+H+ paired sites were more active than single Ga+ sites and the parent H-ZSM-5 catalyst based on a combination of reactivity, quantitative pulse reactions,and DFT calculations.\nThe hypothesis of Ga+H+ pair sites and iso- lated Ga+ species having different reactivities has been put forth in recent investigations by both the Bell and the Lercher groups [9 11,21], however, the existence of these distinct sites is largely indi- rect; inferred from reactivity data, indirect experimental character- izations and computational investigations.", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to a gap between demand and supply, as propylene is traditionally obtained as a by-product from naphtha steam crackers and fluidized catalytic cracking units in refineries. The abundance of natural gas as a feedstock has exacerbated this gap. Propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is seen as a potentially effective alternative method to produce propylene. Two commercialized PDH processes are the Catofin process using a CrOx/Al2O3 catalyst and the Oleflex process with a Pt-based catalyst. However, the high cost of Pt and health and environmental concerns associated with Cr have driven the development of alternative PDH catalysts, such as Ga-, Zn-, Co-, V-based, and ZrO2 catalysts. Among these, Ga/H-ZSM-5 has been recognized as an efficient catalyst for dehydrogenation and dehydroaromatization of alkanes, but the identity of catalytic active sites and the reaction mechanism of PDH remain topics of active discussion. Various experimental techniques, including in-situ Ga K edge X-ray absorption near edge structure (XANES), ex-situ FTIR, and NH3-temperature-programmed desorption (NH3-TPD), have been used to probe Ga speciation in Ga/H-ZSM-5 and identify the active site in PDH. A number of Ga species have been proposed to form after the reduction of Ga/H-ZSM-5, including Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga(OH)]2+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaH2]+, and [GaH]2+. Early X-ray absorption studies suggested that isolated Ga+ ions are the main species in Ga/H-ZSM-5, independent of gallium loading and reducing gas, consistent with a recent report. However, alternative interpretations of edge shifts in Ga K-edge XANES spectra have been proposed, as XANES spectra are not sufficiently resolved to differentiate Ga+ from low-coordinate Ga-alkyl or hydride species. Hensen and coworkers first identified Ga monohydride and dihydride species on reduced Ga/H-ZSM-5 using diffuse reflectance infrared Fourier Transform spectroscopy (DRIFTS), suggesting these species could play an active role in PDH. However, spectra were collected at room temperature after reducing samples with H2 at 500 C, which may not represent the catalyst state at 500 C. Phadke et al. proposed that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active centers for PDH, and catalyst reactivity is independent of Ga/Al ratio, supported by FTIR spectroscopic, NH3-TPD results, and thermodynamic stability analysis. However, FTIR and NH3-TPD experiments were conducted on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in its oxidized state, where Ga speciation could differ from the reduced sample. Schreiber et al. reported that Ga+H+ paired sites were more active than single Ga+ sites and the parent H-ZSM-5 catalyst based on reactivity, quantitative pulse reactions, and DFT calculations. The hypothesis of Ga+H+ pair sites and isolated Ga+ species having different reactivities has been put forth in recent investigations, but the existence of these distinct sites is largely indirect, inferred from reactivity data, indirect experimental characterizations, and computational investigations.", "Chinese": "丙烯在化工基础设施中扮演着核心角色，用于生产包括聚丙烯、丙烯腈、丙烯氧化物和莰烯在内的广泛化学品。目前，丙烯作为副产品，主要来自炼油厂的石脑油蒸汽裂解和流化催化裂解（FCC）单元。然而，由于天然气作为原料的显著增加，丙烯的需求和供应之间出现了日益扩大的差距。丙烷脱氢（PDH）被认为是一种生产丙烯的有效替代方法，两种PDH工艺，即使用CrOx/Al2O3催化剂的Catofin工艺和使用基于Pt的催化剂的Oleflex工艺，已被商业化。然而，由于Pt的高成本以及与Cr相关的健康和环境问题，这推动了其他PDH催化剂的发展，如Ga-、Zn-、Co-、V基和ZrO2催化剂。其中，Ga/H-ZSM-5长期以来被公认为是烷烃脱氢和脱氢芳构化（Cyclar工艺）的有效催化剂，然而，Ga的物种化、催化活性位点的身份以及PDH反应的反应机制仍然是几十年研究的活跃讨论话题。包括原位Ga K边X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）、原位FTIR和NH3-温度程序脱附（NH3-TPD）在内的各种实验技术已被用于探究Ga/H-ZSM-5中的Ga物种化并识别PDH反应中的活性位点。根据几种实验和计算技术，提出了在Ga/H-ZSM-5还原后可能形成的Ga物种，如Ga+、[GaO]+、[Ga(OH)]2+、[Ga(OH)2]+、[GaH2]+和[GaH]2+。早期的X射线吸收研究表明，无论镓的负载量和所用还原气体如何，孤立的Ga+离子是Ga/H-ZSM-5中的主要物种，这与Schreiber等人最近的报告一致。然而，对在反应条件下获得的Ga K边XANES光谱的边缘位移的替代解释已被提出，因为XANES光谱不足以区分Ga+和低配位Ga-烷基或氢化物物种。Hensen及其同事首先使用扩散反射红外傅里叶变换光谱（DRIFTS）在还原的Ga/H-ZSM-5上识别了Ga单氢化物和二氢化物物种，表明这些物种可能在PDH中发挥活性作用。然而，他们在用H2在500°C还原样品后，在室温下收集光谱，而催化剂在室温下的状态可能无法代表500°C时的催化剂状态。Phadke等人最近提出，单个[GaH]2+位点是PDH反应的活性中心，催化剂的活性独立于Ga/Al比。这得到了FTIR光谱、NH3-TPD结果以及热力学稳定性分析的支持。然而，这些研究中的FTIR和NH3-TPD实验是在Ga/H-ZSM-5的氧化状态下进行的，其中Ga的物种化可能与还原样品大不相同。Schreiber等人报告说，Ga+H+配对位点比单个Ga+位点和母体H-ZSM-5催化剂更活跃，这是基于反应性、定量脉冲反应和DFT计算的组合。Ga+H+配对位点和孤立Ga+物种具有不同反应性的假设在Bell和Lercher小组的最近调查中被提出，然而，这些不同位点的存在在很大程度上是间接的，从反应性数据、间接实验表征和计算研究中推断出来。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2020.11.004"},

The Dow Chemical Company forecasted that the demand for propylene will grow at an average annual rate of 2% to 3% by 2035, which is expected to exceed production capacity between 2016 and 2035. The development of dehydrogenation technologies and catalysts has been widely developed, such as propane dehydrogenation (PDH), the methanol-to-olefins (MTO) process, and the FischerTropsch-to-olefins process. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over the years. The active sites of Ga have been debated and strongly affected by the types of supports, preparation methods, and loading amounts. Studies have shown that the active site of Ga2O3 is the Lewis acid site provided by coordinatively unsaturated Ga3+. Recently, Sattler et al. reported trace Pt modified GaOx as efficient catalysts for propane dehydrogenation. DFT calculations predict that Zrcus cations in the lattice of ZrO2 lower the activation barrier of H2 and C3H6 formation from C3H8 by 0.76 eV in comparison with their saturated counterparts. The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), due to the rapid consumption of fossil energy and the inability of traditional propylene production methods to meet increasing demands. PDH technology is considered a promising method for propylene production. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, with ongoing debate about active Ga species. DFT calculations have shown that the activation of propane on the surface of Ga2O3 involves the loss of hydrogen to form hydroxyl groups, but the desorption step of adsorbed hydrogen atoms limits the activity of Ga2O3. Efforts to improve the activity of GaOx-based catalysts have included doping to increase the number of coordinatively unsaturated Ga3+ sites, and the use of trace Pt as a promoter to facilitate hydrogen desorption and recover gallium hydride and/or hydroxide species. H2 pretreatment can also promote the formation of more active GaH species. However, GaOx-based catalysts suffer from significant sintering during continuous regeneration operations, so controlled regeneration is desired to recover their performance. The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), as an alternative to traditional steam cracking. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over time, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Recent research has identified [GaH]2+ ions together with a basic framework oxygen of the Brnsted-acid site as the active sites in the case of Ga species in ZSM-5 zeolites. This has contributed to our current knowledge of these catalysts.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢（PDH），近年来受到了广泛关注。道化学公司预测，到2035年，丙烯需求将以每年2%至3%的平均速度增长，预计2016年至2035年间需求将超过生产能力。脱氢技术的发展和催化剂的开发，如丙烷脱氢（PDH）、甲醇制烯烃（MTO）过程和费托合成制烯烃过程，已经得到了广泛的发展。对于PDH，Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂的理解多年来一直在发展。Ga的活性位点一直存在争议，并且受到载体类型、制备方法和负载量的强烈影响。研究表明，Ga2O3的活性位点是通过不饱和Ga3+提供的路易斯酸位点。最近，Sattler等人报道了微量Pt改性的GaOx作为丙烷脱氢的有效催化剂。DFT计算预测，与饱和对应物相比，ZrO2晶格中的Zrcus阳离子降低了H2和C3H6从C3H8形成时的活化能垒0.76 eV。丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢（PDH），因为化石能源的快速消耗和传统丙烯生产方法无法满足日益增长的需求。PDH技术被认为是丙烯生产的一种有前景的方法。对于PDH中Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂的理解已经发展，关于活性Ga物种的争论仍在继续。DFT计算表明，丙烷在Ga2O3表面的活化涉及氢的损失形成羟基，但吸附氢原子的脱附步骤限制了Ga2O3的活性。为了提高GaOx基催化剂的活性，已经做出了许多努力，包括掺杂以增加配位不饱和Ga3+位点的数量，以及使用微量Pt作为促进剂，以促进氢的脱附和恢复镓氢化物和/或氢氧化物物种。H2预处理还可以促进更活性的GaH物种的形成。然而，GaOx基催化剂在连续再生操作中遭受严重的烧结，因此需要控制再生以恢复其性能。丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢（PDH），作为传统蒸汽裂解的替代方法。对于PDH中Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂的理解随着时间的推移而发展，关于活性Ga物种的争论仍在继续。最近的研究已经确定了在ZSM-5沸石中Ga物种的情况下，[GaH]2+离子与Brnsted酸位点的基本框架氧一起作为活性位点。这为当前对这些催化剂的理解做出了贡献。", "Doi": "10.1039/d0cs00814a"},
{"Quotes": "No quotes provided", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to increased attention on the catalytic dehydrogenation of propane to propylene, as conventional hydrocarbon steam cracking and catalytic cracking processes cannot meet the growing demand. Gallium oxide-based catalysts, including Ga/H-ZSM-5, have been recognized as promising materials for alkane dehydrogenation due to their capability to activate hydrocarbon species and excellent catalytic efficiency. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Recent research has shown that the existence of strong acid sites in the catalyst can lead to more well-dispersed Ga species, which is beneficial for the propane dehydrogenation reaction. The 5Ga2O3/ZSM-5 sample exhibits the highest catalytic activity, possessing the maximum well-dispersed gallium species and high dehydrogenation efficiency gallium ions (Gad+ cations, d < 2). The 5Ga2O3/SBA-15 catalyst exhibits the highest catalytic stability. The support effects of catalysts were also considered to be an important topic. Previous studies reported that the Ga2O3 species were dispersed on different supports including TiO2, MgO, Al2O3, ZrO2, ZSM-5, HZSM-48 and MWW zeolites for alkane dehydrogenation reaction. Many literatures verified that acidity of support evidently influenced the catalytic performance of the supported catalysts. The detailed investigations of different supports on the catalytic performances for Ga2O3-based catalysts are rarely reported, especially with SBA-15 material as support. The dispersion of Ga2O3 species varied with different supports, and the effects of supports on the state of gallium species have not been fully understood, especially the causes of these changes.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长促使人们更加关注丙烷催化脱氢制丙烯，因为传统的烃类蒸汽裂解和催化裂解工艺无法满足日益增长的需求。基于氧化镓的催化剂，包括Ga/H-ZSM-5，由于其能够激活烃类物质并具有优异的催化效率，已被公认为是烷烃脱氢的有前途的材料。对于Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂在PDH中的理解已经发展，关于活性Ga物种的争论仍在继续。最近的研究表明，催化剂中强酸位的存在可以导致更多的分散良好的Ga物种，这对丙烷脱氢反应是有利的。5Ga2O3/ZSM-5样品表现出最高的催化活性，具有最大量的分散良好的镓物种和高脱氢效率的镓离子（Gad+阳离子，d < 2）。5Ga2O3/SBA-15催化剂表现出最高的催化稳定性。催化剂的载体效应也被认为是一个重要的课题。以前的研究报道，Ga2O3物种分散在TiO2、MgO、Al2O3、ZrO2、ZSM-5、HZSM-48和MWW沸石等不同的载体上，用于烷烃脱氢反应。许多文献证实，载体的酸性对负载催化剂的催化性能有明显影响。对于基于Ga2O3的催化剂，不同载体对其催化性能的详细研究很少被报道，特别是在SBA-15材料作为载体的情况下。Ga2O3物种的分散度随不同载体而变化，载体对镓物种状态的影响尚未完全理解，特别是这些变化的原因。", "Doi": "10.1039/c6ra27204e"},

featuring a highly dispersed GaxPt alloy structure, had a long-term stability evident in unchanged propene selectivity (>99%) over the course of a 20 h DDH reaction.\"\n          [8] \"Cybulskis et al. reported that the preparation strategy could greatly influence the structure of Ga/SiO2 catalysts.\"\n          [9] \"Shao et al. established an optimal Ga loading of 5 wt%, reporting an initial propene yield on different supports that followed the trend: Ga/H-ZSM-5 (48%) > Ga/γ-Al2O3 (43%) > Ga/SBA-15 (28%) > Ga/SiO2 (9%).\"\n          [10] \"Schreiber et al. further verified the active sites for MFI supported Ga catalysts with moderate acidity, reporting an optimal Ga/Al ratio of 0.5, which enhanced the dehydrogenation rate.\"\n          [11] \"DFT calculations indicated that the generated LewisBrnsted acid pair is much more active than an isolated Ga+, due to the large increase in Lewis acidity upon protonation of Ga+ by the BAS, which facilitates heterolytic CH bond activation.\"\n          [12] \"The BAS also significantly reduces the activation barrier for H2 elimination by recombination with a hydride.\"", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), as an alternative to traditional steam cracking and fluid catalytic cracking. The discovery of active and selective catalysts is central to the development of these on-purpose technologies. Research into propane dehydrogenation is an ever-growing field, with several review articles available on direct dehydrogenation (DDH), soft oxidation with CO2 (ODH-CO2), and oxidative dehydrogenation (ODH-O2). The scope of this article is to critically review the literature on DDH, ODH-CO2, and ODH-O2 to identify overarching themes and common rules for catalyst design. The environmental and economic aspects of different existing propene production technologies are important considerations when reviewing the feasibility of newer technologies based on dehydrogenation. Green chemistry principles, such as atom economy, the use of toxic chemicals, and the renewability of the feedstock, are especially relevant. The increased interest in direct propane dehydrogenation has been enhanced by the fall in propane price, which is the direct result of the discovery of vast shale gas reserves in North America. Although propane is a minor component in shale gas, it is facile to separate and therefore represents a valuable, but non-renewable source of propane. Increasing public pressure to move away from such non-renewable feedstocks continues to gain momentum, and the propane production industry has responded accordingly. The production of renewable green propane (also called bio-propane and bioLPG) is an emerging sector which is already being operated on a large scale. TotalEnergies operates a bio-refinery in La Mede, which has a design capacity for bio-propane of 25000 tonnes per year. Additionally, Neste recently opened a renewable propane production plant, which will produce 40000 tonnes per year. The propane generated is then sold on to be used in direct propane dehydrogenation. While this is an important start, it represents less than 1% of annual propane capacity. Bio-propane can be produced from the processing of biomass, notably as a side-product in the production of bio-diesel as well as glycerol and other substrates. With increasing pressure to source chemical feedstocks sustainably, we can expect that new interest will focus on renewable and green routes to the key platform chemicals currently required by modern society, and that green propane will play an important role in this. Overall, direct propane dehydrogenation satisfies many principles of green chemistry in comparison to SC and MTO benchmarks: it is highly atom-economic, does not use toxic reactants (or generate toxic by-products) and can in principle, utilise renewable feedstocks. However, in practice dehydrogenation will only be desirable as a means of producing propene if the reaction can operate efficiently, with minimal side-products and maximum yield. These factors are governed by the choice of catalyst, the main focus of the current review. The development of an active, selective and stable catalyst is essential for dehydrogenation to be considered as a viable process in the near- and long-term future.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢（PDH），作为传统蒸汽裂解和流化催化裂解的替代方案。发现活性和选择性催化剂是开发这些目的技术的核心。丙烷脱氢的研究是一个不断增长的领域，目前有几篇关于直接脱氢（DDH）、二氧化碳软氧化（ODH-CO2）和氧化脱氢（ODH-O2）的综述文章。本文的范围是批判性地回顾DDH、ODH-CO2和ODH-O2的文献，以确定催化剂设计的总体主题和共同规则。我们不试图捕捉反应设计和工程的方面，这本身是一个充满活力的研究领域。我们试图通过计算空间时间产率（STY）（以molC3H6 kgcat1 h1为单位）来比较不同子反应中催化剂的性能，这是基于催化剂的初始活性。此外，我们强调了每个反应的环境和工业视角以及工业应用的前景。不同现有丙烯生产技术的环境和经济方面在审查基于脱氢的较新技术的可行性时是重要的考虑因素。绿色化学原则，如原子经济性、有毒化学品的使用和原料的可再生性，尤其相关。直接丙烷脱氢与SC和MTO基准相比，在绿色化学的许多原则方面令人满意：它是高度原子经济的，不使用有毒反应物（或产生有毒副产品），原则上可以利用可再生原料。然而，在实践中，只有当反应能够有效运行，具有最小的副产品和最大产量时，脱氢才是一种理想的丙烯生产方式。这些因素受催化剂选择的支配，这是当前综述的主要焦点。开发活性、选择性和稳定的催化剂对于脱氢在近期和长期未来被视为可行的过程至关重要。", "Doi": "10.1039/d1gc03700e"},
{"Quotes": "", "English": "The increasing world demand for propylene and the current low cost of propane derived from shale gas have renewed interest in the propane dehydrogenation reaction (PDH). Metal cations (Ga+, Zn2+, Co2+, etc.) exchanged in zeolite H-ZSM-5 have shown promising alkane dehydrogenation properties as well: among them, Ga/H-ZSM-5 exhibits high stability and high propylene selectivity (90%) for propane dehydrogenation. Bell and coworkers believe that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active species; however, Schreiber et al. reported that Ga+H+ pair sites are the stable active sites, a model supported by results from our laboratory. Phadke et al. have pointed out that Ga-exchanged species associated with Al-pairs in Ga/H-MFI catalyze both propane and butane dehydrogenation while isolated Ga species did not. They found, however, that both Ga species exhibited similar properties for ethane dehydrogenation. It is thus possible that the reaction mechanism of propane dehydrogenation with the In-CHA catalyst is different from that of ethane dehydrogenation.", "Chinese": "全球对丙烯的需求日益增长，以及从页岩气中提取的丙烷成本低廉，重新激发了人们对丙烷脱氢反应（PDH）的兴趣。金属阳离子（Ga+，Zn2+，Co2+等）在H-ZSM-5沸石中交换，也显示出有前景的烷烃脱氢性能：其中，Ga/H-ZSM-5在丙烷脱氢中表现出高稳定性和高丙烯选择性（90%）。贝尔和他的同事认为，单个[GaH]2+位点是活性位点；然而，施赖伯等人报告说，Ga+H+对位点是稳定的活性位点，这一模型得到了我们实验室结果的支持。帕德克等人指出，与Ga/H-MFI中Al对相关的Ga交换物种催化丙烷和丁烷脱氢，而孤立的Ga物种则没有。然而，他们发现这两种Ga物种在乙烷脱氢方面表现出相似的性质。因此，In-CHA催化剂催化丙烷脱氢的反应机理可能与乙烷脱氢不同。", "Doi": "10.1039/d1sc05866e"},
{"Quotes": "", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), as an alternative to traditional methods such as steam cracking. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over time, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Recent research has contributed to our current knowledge of these catalysts, including the identification of coordinatively unsaturated tetrahedral Ga3+ cations as the active sites for dehydrogenation activity. However, the exact nature of the active sites is still under debate, with some authors proposing the presence of Lewis acid sites, while others suggest the involvement of both Lewis and Brnsted acid sites. The role of CO2 in improving olefin yields has also been studied, with various mechanisms proposed, including the removal of acid sites, coke gasification, and hydrogen removal by the reverse water-gas shift reaction. The addition of promoters, such as potassium, has been shown to reduce coke formation and increase selectivity. The reducibility of Ga2O3 and the effect of hydrogen and steam on the catalyst's activity have also been investigated. The promotion of GaOx-based dehydrogenation catalysts with metals like Pt has been reported to assist hydrogen desorption and facilitate the regeneration of active sites.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢(PDH)，作为传统方法如蒸汽裂解的替代。对于PDH中Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂的理解随着时间的推移而发展，关于活性Ga物种的争论仍在继续。最近的研究为这些催化剂的当前知识做出了贡献，包括确定四面体配位不足的Ga3+阳离子作为脱氢活性位点。然而，活性位点的确切性质仍在争论中，一些作者提出存在Lewis酸位点，而另一些则建议涉及Lewis和Brnsted酸位点。关于CO2提高烯烃产率的作用也进行了研究，提出了各种机制，包括去除酸位点、焦炭气化和通过逆水煤气变换反应去除氢气。添加钾等促进剂已被证明可以减少焦炭形成并提高选择性。Ga2O3的还原性和氢气、蒸汽对催化剂活性的影响也进行了研究。据报道，Pt等金属对GaOx基脱氢催化剂的促进作用有助于氢气解吸，促进活性位点的再生。", "Doi": "10.1021/cr5002436"},

{"Quotes": "", "English": "The literature does not provide information on how the growing demand for propylene has influenced the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), or how the understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, including the ongoing debate about active Ga species and recent research findings that have contributed to our current knowledge of these catalysts. propylene has led to the development of new production methods, including propane dehydrogenation (PDH), to meet the projected shortfall in supply. Propylene is a key chemical used in the production of various materials, such as polypropylene, acrylonitrile, propylene oxide, and cymene. The demand for propylene is expected to increase significantly, from 130 megatons in 2019 to 191 megatons by 2030. To address this demand, on-purpose propylene technologies, including PDH, have been developed. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over time, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Ga-based catalysts have a long history in hydrocarbon processing, with the dehydroaromatization activity of supported gallium oxide being recognized in the 1970s. Since dehydrogenation is the first step in dehydroaromatization, the ability of Ga/H-ZSM-5 to dehydrogenate light alkanes to alkenes was well appreciated. However, the Ga speciation and the structure of active sites on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in dehydrogenation have remained active topics of discussion since its initial discovery without clear resolution. {"Quotes": "Propylene plays a central role in the chemical industry infras- tructure and it is used for the production of a wide range of chem- icals, including polypropylene, acrylonitrile, propylene oxide, and cymene [1]. Propylene is currently obtained as a by-product from naphtha steam crackers and fluidized catalytic cracking (FCC) units in refineries [2]. However, there has been a growing gap between the demand and supply of propylene, due to a marked increase in the abundance of natural gas as a feedstock [3]. Propane dehy- drogenation (PDH) is potentially an effective alternative to produc- ing propylene, and two PDH processes, i.e., the Catofin process with a CrOx/Al2O3 catalyst and the Oleflex process using a Pt-based cat- alyst, have been commercialized [4,5]. The high cost of Pt and the health and environmental concerns associated with Cr, have incen- tivized development of other PDH catalysts [4], such as Ga- [612], Zn- [13], Co- [1416], V-based [17] and ZrO2 [1820] catalysts.\nAmong these, Ga/H-ZSM-5 has long been recognized as an efficient catalyst for both dehydrogenation and dehydroaromatization of alkanes (the Cyclar process), however, Ga speciation, the identity of catalytic active sites and the reaction mechanism of the PDH reaction remain topics of active discussion despite decades of research [911,2123].\nVarious experimental techniques including in-situ Ga K edge X- ray absorption near edge structure (XANES), ex-situ FTIR and NH3- temperature-programmed desorption (NH3-TPD) have been employed to probe Ga speciation in Ga/H-ZSM-5 and identify the active site in the PDH reaction [911,24].\nA number of Ga species, such as Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga (OH)]2+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaH2]+, [GaH]2+, have been proposed to form after the reduction of Ga/H-ZSM-5 based on several experimental and computational techniques [911,24,2628].\nEarly in-situ X-ray absorption study showed that isolated Ga+ ions are the main species in Ga/H-ZSM-5 independent of the gallium loading and the utilized reducing gas [24,29], which is consistent with a more recent report by Schreiber et al. [10] Alternative interpretations of edge shifts in Ga K-edge XANES spectra acquired under reaction conditions have been proposed, as XANES spectra are not suffi- ciently resolved to differentiate Ga+ from low-coordinate Ga-alkyl or hydride species [11,30].\nHensen and coworkers [27,28] first identified Ga monohydride and dihydride species on reduced Ga/ H-ZSM-5 with diffuse reflectance infrared Fourier Transform spec- troscopy (DRIFTS), suggesting that these species could play an active role in the PDH.\nHowever, they collected spectra at room temperature after reducing samples with H2 at 500 C, and the state of the catalyst at room temperature after cooling may not be representative of the catalyst state at 500 C.\nRecently, Phadke et al. [9] proposed that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active centers for the PDH reaction, and the catalysts reactivity is independent of Ga/Al ratio.\nThis was supported by FTIR spectroscopic and NH3-TPD results, along with thermodynamic stability analysis [11].\nFTIR and NH3-TPD experiments in these studies were con- ducted on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in its oxidized state [11], where the Ga spe- ciation could be quite different from that of the reduced sample.\nSchreiber et al. [10] reported that the Ga+H+ paired sites were more active than single Ga+ sites and the parent H-ZSM-5 catalyst based on a combination of reactivity, quantitative pulse reactions,and DFT calculations.\nThe hypothesis of Ga+H+ pair sites and iso- lated Ga+ species having different reactivities has been put forth in recent investigations by both the Bell and the Lercher groups [9 11,21], however, the existence of these distinct sites is largely indi- rect; inferred from reactivity data, indirect experimental character- izations and computational investigations.", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to a gap between demand and supply, as propylene is traditionally obtained as a by-product from naphtha steam crackers and fluidized catalytic cracking units in refineries. The abundance of natural gas as a feedstock has exacerbated this gap. Propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is seen as a potentially effective alternative method to produce propylene. Two commercialized PDH processes are the Catofin process using a CrOx/Al2O3 catalyst and the Oleflex process with a Pt-based catalyst. However, the high cost of Pt and health and environmental concerns associated with Cr have driven the development of alternative PDH catalysts, such as Ga-, Zn-, Co-, V-based, and ZrO2 catalysts. Among these, Ga/H-ZSM-5 has been recognized as an efficient catalyst for dehydrogenation and dehydroaromatization of alkanes, but the identity of catalytic active sites and the reaction mechanism of PDH remain topics of active discussion. Various experimental techniques, including in-situ Ga K edge X-ray absorption near edge structure (XANES), ex-situ FTIR, and NH3-temperature-programmed desorption (NH3-TPD), have been used to probe Ga speciation in Ga/H-ZSM-5 and identify the active site in PDH. A number of Ga species have been proposed to form after the reduction of Ga/H-ZSM-5, including Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga(OH)]2+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaH2]+, and [GaH]2+. Early X-ray absorption studies suggested that isolated Ga+ ions are the main species in Ga/H-ZSM-5, independent of gallium loading and reducing gas, consistent with a recent report. However, alternative interpretations of edge shifts in Ga K-edge XANES spectra have been proposed, as XANES spectra are not sufficiently resolved to differentiate Ga+ from low-coordinate Ga-alkyl or hydride species. Hensen and coworkers first identified Ga monohydride and dihydride species on reduced Ga/H-ZSM-5 using diffuse reflectance infrared Fourier Transform spectroscopy (DRIFTS), suggesting these species could play an active role in PDH. However, spectra were collected at room temperature after reducing samples with H2 at 500 C, which may not represent the catalyst state at 500 C. Phadke et al. proposed that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active centers for PDH, and catalyst reactivity is independent of Ga/Al ratio, supported by FTIR spectroscopic, NH3-TPD results, and thermodynamic stability analysis. However, FTIR and NH3-TPD experiments were conducted on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in its oxidized state, where Ga speciation could differ from the reduced sample. Schreiber et al. reported that Ga+H+ paired sites were more active than single Ga+ sites and the parent H-ZSM-5 catalyst based on reactivity, quantitative pulse reactions, and DFT calculations. The hypothesis of Ga+H+ pair sites and isolated Ga+ species having different reactivities has been put forth in recent investigations, but the existence of these distinct sites is largely indirect, inferred from reactivity data, indirect experimental characterizations, and computational investigations.", "Chinese": "丙烯在化工基础设施中扮演着核心角色，用于生产包括聚丙烯、丙烯腈、丙烯氧化物和莰烯在内的广泛化学品。目前，丙烯作为副产品，主要来自炼油厂的石脑油蒸汽裂解和流化催化裂解（FCC）单元。然而，由于天然气作为原料的显著增加，丙烯的需求和供应之间出现了日益扩大的差距。丙烷脱氢（PDH）被认为是一种生产丙烯的有效替代方法，两种PDH工艺，即使用CrOx/Al2O3催化剂的Catofin工艺和使用基于Pt的催化剂的Oleflex工艺，已被商业化。然而，由于Pt的高成本以及与Cr相关的健康和环境问题，这推动了其他PDH催化剂的发展，如Ga-、Zn-、Co-、V基和ZrO2催化剂。其中，Ga/H-ZSM-5长期以来被公认为是烷烃脱氢和脱氢芳构化（Cyclar工艺）的有效催化剂，然而，Ga的物种化、催化活性位点的身份以及PDH反应的反应机制仍然是几十年研究的活跃讨论话题。包括原位Ga K边X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）、原位FTIR和NH3-温度程序脱附（NH3-TPD）在内的各种实验技术已被用于探究Ga/H-ZSM-5中的Ga物种化并识别PDH反应中的活性位点。根据几种实验和计算技术，提出了在Ga/H-ZSM-5还原后可能形成的Ga物种，如Ga+、[GaO]+、[Ga(OH)]2+、[Ga(OH)2]+、[GaH2]+和[GaH]2+。早期的X射线吸收研究表明，无论镓的负载量和所用还原气体如何，孤立的Ga+离子是Ga/H-ZSM-5中的主要物种，这与Schreiber等人最近的报告一致。然而，对在反应条件下获得的Ga K边XANES光谱的边缘位移的替代解释已被提出，因为XANES光谱不足以区分Ga+和低配位Ga-烷基或氢化物物种。Hensen及其同事首先使用扩散反射红外傅里叶变换光谱（DRIFTS）在还原的Ga/H-ZSM-5上识别了Ga单氢化物和二氢化物物种，表明这些物种可能在PDH中发挥活性作用。然而，他们在用H2在500°C还原样品后，在室温下收集光谱，而催化剂在室温下的状态可能无法代表500°C时的催化剂状态。Phadke等人最近提出，单个[GaH]2+位点是PDH反应的活性中心，催化剂的活性独立于Ga/Al比。这得到了FTIR光谱、NH3-TPD结果以及热力学稳定性分析的支持。然而，这些研究中的FTIR和NH3-TPD实验是在Ga/H-ZSM-5的氧化状态下进行的，其中Ga的物种化可能与还原样品大不相同。Schreiber等人报告说，Ga+H+配对位点比单个Ga+位点和母体H-ZSM-5催化剂更活跃，这是基于反应性、定量脉冲反应和DFT计算的组合。Ga+H+配对位点和孤立Ga+物种具有不同反应性的假设在Bell和Lercher小组的最近调查中被提出，然而，这些不同位点的存在在很大程度上是间接的，从反应性数据、间接实验表征和计算研究中推断出来。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2020.11.004"},

The Dow Chemical Company forecasted that the demand for propylene will grow at an average annual rate of 2% to 3% by 2035, which is expected to exceed production capacity between 2016 and 2035. The development of dehydrogenation technologies and catalysts has been widely developed, such as propane dehydrogenation (PDH), the methanol-to-olefins (MTO) process, and the FischerTropsch-to-olefins process. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over the years. The active sites of Ga have been debated and strongly affected by the types of supports, preparation methods, and loading amounts. Studies have shown that the active site of Ga2O3 is the Lewis acid site provided by coordinatively unsaturated Ga3+. Recently, Sattler et al. reported trace Pt modified GaOx as efficient catalysts for propane dehydrogenation. DFT calculations predict that Zrcus cations in the lattice of ZrO2 lower the activation barrier of H2 and C3H6 formation from C3H8 by 0.76 eV in comparison with their saturated counterparts. The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), due to the rapid consumption of fossil energy and the inability of traditional propylene production methods to meet increasing demands. PDH technology is considered a promising method for propylene production. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, with ongoing debate about active Ga species. DFT calculations have shown that the activation of propane on the surface of Ga2O3 involves the loss of hydrogen to form hydroxyl groups, but the desorption step of adsorbed hydrogen atoms limits the activity of Ga2O3. Efforts to improve the activity of GaOx-based catalysts have included doping to increase the number of coordinatively unsaturated Ga3+ sites, and the use of trace Pt as a promoter to facilitate hydrogen desorption and recover gallium hydride and/or hydroxide species. H2 pretreatment can also promote the formation of more active GaH species. However, GaOx-based catalysts suffer from significant sintering during continuous regeneration operations, so controlled regeneration is desired to recover their performance. The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), as an alternative to traditional steam cracking. Recent research has identified [GaH]2+ ions together with a basic framework oxygen of the Brnsted-acid site as the active sites in the case of Ga species in ZSM-5 zeolites. {"Quotes": "No quotes provided", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to increased attention on the catalytic dehydrogenation of propane to propylene, as conventional hydrocarbon steam cracking and catalytic cracking processes cannot meet the growing demand. Gallium oxide-based catalysts, including Ga/H-ZSM-5, have been recognized as promising materials for alkane dehydrogenation due to their capability to activate hydrocarbon species and excellent catalytic efficiency. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Recent research has shown that the existence of strong acid sites in the catalyst can lead to more well-dispersed Ga species, which is beneficial for the propane dehydrogenation reaction. The 5Ga2O3/ZSM-5 sample exhibits the highest catalytic activity, possessing the maximum well-dispersed gallium species and high dehydrogenation efficiency gallium ions (Gad+ cations, d < 2). The 5Ga2O3/SBA-15 catalyst exhibits the highest catalytic stability. The support effects of catalysts were also considered to be an important topic. Previous studies reported that the Ga2O3 species were dispersed on different supports including TiO2, MgO, Al2O3, ZrO2, ZSM-5, HZSM-48 and MWW zeolites for alkane dehydrogenation reaction. Many literatures verified that acidity of support evidently influenced the catalytic performance of the supported catalysts. The detailed investigations of different supports on the catalytic performances for Ga2O3-based catalysts are rarely reported, especially with SBA-15 material as support. The dispersion of Ga2O3 species varied with different supports, and the effects of supports on the state of gallium species have not been fully understood, especially the causes of these changes.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长促使人们更加关注丙烷催化脱氢制丙烯，因为传统的烃类蒸汽裂解和催化裂解工艺无法满足日益增长的需求。基于氧化镓的催化剂，包括Ga/H-ZSM-5，由于其能够激活烃类物质并具有优异的催化效率，已被公认为是烷烃脱氢的有前途的材料。对于Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂在PDH中的理解已经发展，关于活性Ga物种的争论仍在继续。最近的研究表明，催化剂中强酸位的存在可以导致更多的分散良好的Ga物种，这对丙烷脱氢反应是有利的。5Ga2O3/ZSM-5样品表现出最高的催化活性，具有最大量的分散良好的镓物种和高脱氢效率的镓离子（Gad+阳离子，d < 2）。5Ga2O3/SBA-15催化剂表现出最高的催化稳定性。催化剂的载体效应也被认为是一个重要的课题。以前的研究报道，Ga2O3物种分散在TiO2、MgO、Al2O3、ZrO2、ZSM-5、HZSM-48和MWW沸石等不同的载体上，用于烷烃脱氢反应。许多文献证实，载体的酸性对负载催化剂的催化性能有明显影响。对于基于Ga2O3的催化剂，不同载体对其催化性能的详细研究很少被报道，特别是在SBA-15材料作为载体的情况下。Ga2O3物种的分散度随不同载体而变化，载体对镓物种状态的影响尚未完全理解，特别是这些变化的原因。", "Doi": "10.1039/c6ra27204e"},

propene yield on different supports that followed the trend: Ga/H-ZSM-5 (48%) > Ga/γ-Al2O3 (43%) > Ga/SBA-15 (28%) > Ga/SiO2 (9%).\"\n          [10] \"Schreiber et al. further verified the active generated LewisBrnsted acid pair is much more active than an isolated Ga+, due to the large increase in Lewis acidity upon protonation of Ga+ by the BAS, which facilitates heterolytic CH bond activation.\"\n          [12] \"The BAS also significantly reduces the activation barrier for H2 elimination by recombination with a hydride.\"", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), as an alternative to traditional steam cracking and fluid catalytic cracking. The discovery of active and selective catalysts is central to the development of these on-purpose technologies. Research into propane dehydrogenation is an ever-growing field, with several review articles available on direct dehydrogenation (DDH), soft oxidation with CO2 (ODH-CO2), and oxidative dehydrogenation (ODH-O2). The scope of this article is to critically review the literature on DDH, ODH-CO2, and ODH-O2 to identify overarching themes and common rules for catalyst design. The environmental and economic aspects of different existing propene production technologies are important considerations when reviewing the feasibility of newer technologies based on dehydrogenation. Green chemistry principles, such as atom economy, the use of toxic chemicals, and the renewability of the feedstock, are especially relevant. The increased interest in direct propane dehydrogenation has been enhanced by the fall in propane price, which is the direct result of the discovery of vast shale gas reserves in North America. Although propane is a minor component in shale gas, it is facile to separate and therefore represents a valuable, but non-renewable source of propane. Increasing public pressure to move away from such non-renewable feedstocks continues to gain momentum, and the propane production industry has responded accordingly. The production of renewable green propane (also called bio-propane and bioLPG) is an emerging sector which is already being operated on a large scale. TotalEnergies operates a bio-refinery in La Mede, which has a design capacity for bio-propane of 25000 tonnes per year. Additionally, Neste recently opened a renewable propane production plant, which will produce 40000 tonnes per year. The propane generated is then sold on to be used in direct propane dehydrogenation. While this is an important start, it represents less than 1% of annual propane capacity. Bio-propane can be produced from the processing of biomass, notably as a side-product in the production of bio-diesel as well as glycerol and other substrates. With increasing pressure to source chemical feedstocks sustainably, we can expect that new interest will focus on renewable and green routes to the key platform chemicals currently required by modern society, and that green propane will play an important role in this. Overall, direct propane dehydrogenation satisfies many principles of green chemistry in comparison to SC and MTO benchmarks: it is highly atom-economic, does not use toxic reactants (or generate toxic by-products) and can in principle, utilise renewable feedstocks. However, in practice dehydrogenation will only be desirable as a means of producing propene if the reaction can operate efficiently, with minimal side-products and maximum yield. These factors are governed by the choice of catalyst, the main focus of the current review. The development of an active, selective and stable catalyst is essential for dehydrogenation to be considered as a viable process in the near- and long-term future.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢（PDH），作为传统蒸汽裂解和流化催化裂解的替代方案。发现活性和选择性催化剂是开发这些目的技术的核心。丙烷脱氢的研究是一个不断增长的领域，目前有几篇关于直接脱氢（DDH）、二氧化碳软氧化（ODH-CO2）和氧化脱氢（ODH-O2）的综述文章。本文的范围是批判性地回顾DDH、ODH-CO2和ODH-O2的文献，以确定催化剂设计的总体主题和共同规则。我们不试图捕捉反应设计和工程的方面，这本身是一个充满活力的研究领域。我们试图通过计算空间时间产率（STY）（以molC3H6 kgcat1 h1为单位）来比较不同子反应中催化剂的性能，这是基于催化剂的初始活性。此外，我们强调了每个反应的环境和工业视角以及工业应用的前景。不同现有丙烯生产技术的环境和经济方面在审查基于脱氢的较新技术的可行性时是重要的考虑因素。绿色化学原则，如原子经济性、有毒化学品的使用和原料的可再生性，尤其相关。直接丙烷脱氢与SC和MTO基准相比，在绿色化学的许多原则方面令人满意：它是高度原子经济的，不使用有毒反应物（或产生有毒副产品），原则上可以利用可再生原料。然而，在实践中，只有当反应能够有效运行，具有最小的副产品和最大产量时，脱氢才是一种理想的丙烯生产方式。这些因素受催化剂选择的支配，这是当前综述的主要焦点。开发活性、选择性和稳定的催化剂对于脱氢在近期和长期未来被视为可行的过程至关重要。", "Doi": "10.1039/d1gc03700e"},
{"Quotes": "", "English": "The increasing world demand for propylene and the current low cost of propane derived from shale gas have renewed interest in the propane dehydrogenation reaction (PDH). Bell and coworkers believe that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active species; however, Schreiber et al. reported that Ga+H+ pair sites are the stable active sites, a model supported by results from our laboratory. Phadke et al. have pointed out that Ga-exchanged species associated with Al-pairs in Ga/H-MFI catalyze both propane and butane dehydrogenation while isolated Ga species did not. They found, however, that both Ga species exhibited similar properties for ethane dehydrogenation. {"Quotes": "", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to the development of new production methods, particularly propane dehydrogenation (PDH), as an alternative to traditional methods such as steam cracking. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over time, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Recent research has contributed to our current knowledge of these catalysts, including the identification of coordinatively unsaturated tetrahedral Ga3+ cations as the active sites for dehydrogenation activity. However, the exact nature of the active sites is still under debate, with some authors proposing the presence of Lewis acid sites, while others suggest the involvement of both Lewis and Brnsted acid sites. The role of CO2 in improving olefin yields has also been studied, with various mechanisms proposed, including the removal of acid sites, coke gasification, and hydrogen removal by the reverse water-gas shift reaction. The addition of promoters, such as potassium, has been shown to reduce coke formation and increase selectivity. The reducibility of Ga2O3 and the effect of hydrogen and steam on the catalyst's activity have also been investigated. The promotion of GaOx-based dehydrogenation catalysts with metals like Pt has been reported to assist hydrogen desorption and facilitate the regeneration of active sites.", "Chinese": "丙烯需求的不断增长推动了新的生产方法的发展，特别是丙烷脱氢(PDH)，作为传统方法如蒸汽裂解的替代。对于PDH中Ga/H-ZSM-5催化剂的理解随着时间的推移而发展，关于活性Ga物种的争论仍在继续。最近的研究为这些催化剂的当前知识做出了贡献，包括确定四面体配位不足的Ga3+阳离子作为脱氢活性位点。然而，活性位点的确切性质仍在争论中，一些作者提出存在Lewis酸位点，而另一些则建议涉及Lewis和Brnsted酸位点。关于CO2提高烯烃产率的作用也进行了研究，提出了各种机制，包括去除酸位点、焦炭气化和通过逆水煤气变换反应去除氢气。添加钾等促进剂已被证明可以减少焦炭形成并提高选择性。Ga2O3的还原性和氢气、蒸汽对催化剂活性的影响也进行了研究。据报道，Pt等金属对GaOx基脱氢催化剂的促进作用有助于氢气解吸，促进活性位点的再生。", "Doi": "10.1021/cr5002436"},

propylene has led to the development of new production methods, including propane dehydrogenation (PDH), to meet the projected shortfall in supply. Propylene is a key chemical used in the production of various materials, such as polypropylene, acrylonitrile, propylene oxide, and cymene. The demand for propylene is expected to increase significantly, from 130 megatons in 2019 to 191 megatons by 2030. To address this demand, on-purpose propylene technologies, including PDH, have been developed. The understanding of Ga/H-ZSM-5 catalysts for PDH has evolved over time, with ongoing debate about the active Ga species. Ga-based catalysts have a long history in hydrocarbon processing, with the dehydroaromatization activity of supported gallium oxide being recognized in the 1970s. Since dehydrogenation is the first step in dehydroaromatization, the ability of Ga/H-ZSM-5 to dehydrogenate light alkanes to alkenes was well appreciated. However, the Ga speciation and the structure of active sites on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in dehydrogenation have remained active topics of discussion since its initial discovery without clear resolution. Different Ga species have been proposed to be the active center of the PDH, including Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaOH]2+, [GaH]2+, [GaH2]+, and Ga+H+ pair. {"Quotes": "Propylene plays a central role in the chemical industry infras- tructure and it is used for the production of a wide range of chem- icals, including polypropylene, acrylonitrile, propylene oxide, and cymene [1]. Propylene is currently obtained as a by-product from naphtha steam crackers and fluidized catalytic cracking (FCC) units in refineries [2]. However, there has been a growing gap between the demand and supply of propylene, due to a marked increase in the abundance of natural gas as a feedstock [3]. Propane dehy- drogenation (PDH) is potentially an effective alternative to produc- ing propylene, and two PDH processes, i.e., the Catofin process with a CrOx/Al2O3 catalyst and the Oleflex process using a Pt-based cat- alyst, have been commercialized [4,5]. The high cost of Pt and the health and environmental concerns associated with Cr, have incen- tivized development of other PDH catalysts [4], such as Ga- [612], Zn- [13], Co- [1416], V-based [17] and ZrO2 [1820] catalysts.\nAmong these, Ga/H-ZSM-5 has long been recognized as an efficient catalyst for both dehydrogenation and dehydroaromatization of alkanes (the Cyclar process), however, Ga speciation, the identity of catalytic active sites and the reaction mechanism of the PDH reaction remain topics of active discussion despite decades of research [911,2123].\nVarious experimental techniques including in-situ Ga K edge X- ray absorption near edge structure (XANES), ex-situ FTIR and NH3- temperature-programmed desorption (NH3-TPD) have been employed to probe Ga speciation in Ga/H-ZSM-5 and identify the active site in the PDH reaction [911,24].\nA number of Ga species, such as Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga (OH)]2+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaH2]+, [GaH]2+, have been proposed to form after the reduction of Ga/H-ZSM-5 based on several experimental and computational techniques [911,24,2628].\nEarly in-situ X-ray absorption study showed that isolated Ga+ ions are the main species in Ga/H-ZSM-5 independent of the gallium loading and the utilized reducing gas [24,29], which is consistent with a more recent report by Schreiber et al. [10] Alternative interpretations of edge shifts in Ga K-edge XANES spectra acquired under reaction conditions have been proposed, as XANES spectra are not suffi- ciently resolved to differentiate Ga+ from low-coordinate Ga-alkyl or hydride species [11,30].\nHensen and coworkers [27,28] first identified Ga monohydride and dihydride species on reduced Ga/ H-ZSM-5 with diffuse reflectance infrared Fourier Transform spec- troscopy (DRIFTS), suggesting that these species could play an active role in the PDH.\nHowever, they collected spectra at room temperature after reducing samples with H2 at 500 C, and the state of the catalyst at room temperature after cooling may not be representative of the catalyst state at 500 C.\nRecently, Phadke et al. [9] proposed that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active centers for the PDH reaction, and the catalysts reactivity is independent of Ga/Al ratio.\nThis was supported by FTIR spectroscopic and NH3-TPD results, along with thermodynamic stability analysis [11].\nFTIR and NH3-TPD experiments in these studies were con- ducted on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in its oxidized state [11], where the Ga spe- ciation could be quite different from that of the reduced sample.\nSchreiber et al. [10] reported that the Ga+H+ paired sites were more active than single Ga+ sites and the parent H-ZSM-5 catalyst based on a combination of reactivity, quantitative pulse reactions,and DFT calculations.\nThe hypothesis of Ga+H+ pair sites and iso- lated Ga+ species having different reactivities has been put forth in recent investigations by both the Bell and the Lercher groups [9 11,21], however, the existence of these distinct sites is largely indi- rect; inferred from reactivity data, indirect experimental character- izations and computational investigations.", "English": "The growing demand for propylene has led to a gap between demand and supply, as propylene is traditionally obtained as a by-product from naphtha steam crackers and fluidized catalytic cracking units in refineries. The abundance of natural gas as a feedstock has exacerbated this gap. Propane dehydrogenation (PDH) is seen as a potentially effective alternative method to produce propylene. Two commercialized PDH processes are the Catofin process using a CrOx/Al2O3 catalyst and the Oleflex process with a Pt-based catalyst. However, the high cost of Pt and health and environmental concerns associated with Cr have driven the development of alternative PDH catalysts, such as Ga-, Zn-, Co-, V-based, and ZrO2 catalysts. Among these, Ga/H-ZSM-5 has been recognized as an efficient catalyst for dehydrogenation and dehydroaromatization of alkanes, but the identity of catalytic active sites and the reaction mechanism of PDH remain topics of active discussion. Various experimental techniques, including in-situ Ga K edge X-ray absorption near edge structure (XANES), ex-situ FTIR, and NH3-temperature-programmed desorption (NH3-TPD), have been used to probe Ga speciation in Ga/H-ZSM-5 and identify the active site in PDH. A number of Ga species have been proposed to form after the reduction of Ga/H-ZSM-5, including Ga+, [GaO]+, [Ga(OH)]2+, [Ga(OH)2]+, [GaH2]+, and [GaH]2+. Early X-ray absorption studies suggested that isolated Ga+ ions are the main species in Ga/H-ZSM-5, independent of gallium loading and reducing gas, consistent with a recent report. However, alternative interpretations of edge shifts in Ga K-edge XANES spectra have been proposed, as XANES spectra are not sufficiently resolved to differentiate Ga+ from low-coordinate Ga-alkyl or hydride species. Hensen and coworkers first identified Ga monohydride and dihydride species on reduced Ga/H-ZSM-5 using diffuse reflectance infrared Fourier Transform spectroscopy (DRIFTS), suggesting these species could play an active role in PDH. However, spectra were collected at room temperature after reducing samples with H2 at 500 C, which may not represent the catalyst state at 500 C. Phadke et al. proposed that single [GaH]2+ sites are the active centers for PDH, and catalyst reactivity is independent of Ga/Al ratio, supported by FTIR spectroscopic, NH3-TPD results, and thermodynamic stability analysis. However, FTIR and NH3-TPD experiments were conducted on Ga/H-ZSM-5 in its oxidized state, where Ga speciation could differ from the reduced sample. Schreiber et al. reported that Ga+H+ paired sites were more active than single Ga+ sites and the parent H-ZSM-5 catalyst based on reactivity, quantitative pulse reactions, and DFT calculations. The hypothesis of Ga+H+ pair sites and isolated Ga+ species having different reactivities has been put forth in recent investigations, but the existence of these distinct sites is largely indirect, inferred from reactivity data, indirect experimental characterizations, and computational investigations.", "Chinese": "丙烯在化工基础设施中扮演着核心角色，用于生产包括聚丙烯、丙烯腈、丙烯氧化物和莰烯在内的广泛化学品。目前，丙烯作为副产品，主要来自炼油厂的石脑油蒸汽裂解和流化催化裂解（FCC）单元。然而，由于天然气作为原料的显著增加，丙烯的需求和供应之间出现了日益扩大的差距。丙烷脱氢（PDH）被认为是一种生产丙烯的有效替代方法，两种PDH工艺，即使用CrOx/Al2O3催化剂的Catofin工艺和使用基于Pt的催化剂的Oleflex工艺，已被商业化。然而，由于Pt的高成本以及与Cr相关的健康和环境问题，这推动了其他PDH催化剂的发展，如Ga-、Zn-、Co-、V基和ZrO2催化剂。其中，Ga/H-ZSM-5长期以来被公认为是烷烃脱氢和脱氢芳构化（Cyclar工艺）的有效催化剂，然而，Ga的物种化、催化活性位点的身份以及PDH反应的反应机制仍然是几十年研究的活跃讨论话题。包括原位Ga K边X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）、原位FTIR和NH3-温度程序脱附（NH3-TPD）在内的各种实验技术已被用于探究Ga/H-ZSM-5中的Ga物种化并识别PDH反应中的活性位点。根据几种实验和计算技术，提出了在Ga/H-ZSM-5还原后可能形成的Ga物种，如Ga+、[GaO]+、[Ga(OH)]2+、[Ga(OH)2]+、[GaH2]+和[GaH]2+。早期的X射线吸收研究表明，无论镓的负载量和所用还原气体如何，孤立的Ga+离子是Ga/H-ZSM-5中的主要物种，这与Schreiber等人最近的报告一致。然而，对在反应条件下获得的Ga K边XANES光谱的边缘位移的替代解释已被提出，因为XANES光谱不足以区分Ga+和低配位Ga-烷基或氢化物物种。Hensen及其同事首先使用扩散反射红外傅里叶变换光谱（DRIFTS）在还原的Ga/H-ZSM-5上识别了Ga单氢化物和二氢化物物种，表明这些物种可能在PDH中发挥活性作用。然而，他们在用H2在500°C还原样品后，在室温下收集光谱，而催化剂在室温下的状态可能无法代表500°C时的催化剂状态。Phadke等人最近提出，单个[GaH]2+位点是PDH反应的活性中心，催化剂的活性独立于Ga/Al比。这得到了FTIR光谱、NH3-TPD结果以及热力学稳定性分析的支持。然而，这些研究中的FTIR和NH3-TPD实验是在Ga/H-ZSM-5的氧化状态下进行的，其中Ga的物种化可能与还原样品大不相同。Schreiber等人报告说，Ga+H+配对位点比单个Ga+位点和母体H-ZSM-5催化剂更活跃，这是基于反应性、定量脉冲反应和DFT计算的组合。Ga+H+配对位点和孤立Ga+物种具有不同反应性的假设在Bell和Lercher小组的最近调查中被提出，然而，这些不同位点的存在在很大程度上是间接的，从反应性数据、间接实验表征和计算研究中推断出来。", "Doi": "10.1016/j.jcat.2020.11.004"},
